  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_6ab8a6b8-8e04-4293-bd4a-7cb3b76835ae'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer16406957610724736121"><b>The second part in The Blackstone Affair series!<br/> <br/>Looming danger. A love worth fighting for. A man who’ll go all in.</b><br/><br/>Ethan Blackstone has a problem on his hands. He’s broken Brynne’s trust and she’s left him.   <span id="freeText16406957610724736121" style="display:none"><b>The second part in The Blackstone Affair series!<br /> <br />Looming danger. A love worth fighting for. A man who’ll go all in.</b><br /><br />Ethan Blackstone has a problem on his hands. He’s broken Brynne’s trust and she’s left him. He’s unwilling to live without her and isn’t giving up—he’s dead-set on getting his beautiful American girl back. The passion between them was explosive, but the secrets they hid from each other are dark and chilling and are powerful enough to destroy their shot at a life together. With political threats now directed at Brynne, Ethan is running out of time and he’ll need to gather all his strength and agility to protect her from the dangers that could take her away from him forever. Will Ethan be able to save Brynne from a past that keeps her locked in fear? Will he ever feel the warmth of her touch, the solidity of her trust again? This is a love-struck man who is willing to do whatever it takes to possess the heart of the woman he loves. He’ll go to any lengths to protect her. He’ll go all in.<br /><br />Here is the fiery story of what happens when two people surrender to a love so great it can heal the scars of the past and give way to a life of pure, rapturous ecstasy.</span>

    <div class="section firstReview">
      

<div id="review_413321360" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/413321360" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/413321360?book_show_action=true">Sep 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=abused-heroine">abused-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=alpha-hero">alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=shower-smexin">shower-smexin</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=super-rich-hero">super-rich-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=scarred-heroes">scarred-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=tortured-abused-hero">tortured-abused-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=cover-lust-i-has-it">cover-lust-i-has-it</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer413321360" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17012245511514751486"><b>
  <blockquote>Stop all the clocks, cut off the telephone,<br/>Prevent the dog from barking with a juicy bone</blockquote>
</b><br/><br/><a href='http://photobucket.com' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391053ra/753135.gif' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>At last, one of the most hotly anticipated sequels of the year is finally here and it’s another sexy read, probably about twice as long as Naked and, interestingly, told entirely from Ethan’s POV.<br/><br/>We pick up exactly where we left them at the end of Naked with Brynne running from Ethan and Ethan losing his head in rage and grief and regret. He’s a broken man at the beginning of this one, a wretched cre</span>
  <span id="freeText17012245511514751486" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>Stop all the clocks, cut off the telephone,<br>Prevent the dog from barking with a juicy bone</blockquote>
</b><br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391053ra/753135.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>At last, one of the most hotly anticipated sequels of the year is finally here and it’s another sexy read, probably about twice as long as Naked and, interestingly, told entirely from Ethan’s POV.<br><br>We pick up exactly where we left them at the end of Naked with Brynne running from Ethan and Ethan losing his head in rage and grief and regret. He’s a broken man at the beginning of this one, a wretched creature without Brynne. His exile from her has forced him into utter desolation.<br><br>He does, of course, manage to win her back and most of the novel is dedicated to the progression of their relationship told from his very possessive and protective POV. It’s very intriguing to get inside the head of an alpha-male like this, to see what makes him tick and what motivates him. Ethan is a man obsessed, his every waking minute and some of his dreams are consumed by Brynne and his fears for her safety and he can’t imagine life without her now. She is his Aphrodite and he her Eros. Ethan and his American Beauty.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote> I don’t know any other way to be with you. It’s all in for me. And I want it to be all in for you too.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>We get to learn the secret that has tortured Brynne for so long and it’s a real shocker. I could only feel profound sadness for what she’s had to endure. Ethan’s past is also revealed and the poor man has really suffered but he still isn’t at the point where he can share all of that with Brynne.<br><br>It’s a very erotic tale as their passion burns white hot and they light up the pages of this novel with their frequent lovemaking scenes. Ethan maybe filthy between the sheets but he’s also a real gentleman with Brynne and I had a real thing for the way he kept kissing her hand. Le sigh!<br><br><a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380391053i/753136.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I did feel, after their reconciliation, that their story began to lack direction and I didn’t fully see the threat to Brynne or where Raine Miller intends to take the story next. There’s no cliffhanger at the end of this one but certain elements of the story are left unresolved and things unsaid.<br><br>I had to have a giggle at the dig Ethan makes against the Fifty Shades books. Sure, they’re not mentioned by name but it’s obvious what Brynne and Gabrielle are cooing over.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote> I mean, who reads this crap? Who has time? Why even read about sex in a book when you can have it instead? I don’t get that. And billionaires in their twenties? I mentally shook my head and pretended to care. I’m such a bastard.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>So, this book is mostly just an erotic romance, the rest of the plot doesn’t really move much further in this one. I developed a real fondness for Muriel, the toothy newspaper hag who, when she spoke, kind of reminded of an extra from My Fair Lady with her exaggerated cockney! There’s obviously going to be a connection between Ivan and Gabrielle – perhaps they will get their own story eventually. As a Brit myself, I felt that this had a better British feel to it compared to Naked. Ethan uses all the right slang and it didn't feel at all Americanised which is how I felt when I read Naked.<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I am totally not sold on the epilogue being told from the POV of Ethan’s fish. I’m hoping that this is not going to be the case for book 3! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>4 stars contemporary romance<br><br>The Lovely Ethan<br><br><a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380391053i/753137._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><i>For more reviews, please visit <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Reviews</a></i><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_413229086" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Debbie " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5667316-debbie"><img alt="Debbie " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1550465070p2/5667316.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/413229086?book_show_action=true">Sep 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debbie " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debbie " href="/user/show/5667316-debbie">Debbie </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5667316-debbie?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5667316-debbie?shelf=anxiously-waiting-for">anxiously-waiting-for</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer413229086" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13617231355172781608"><b>
  <a href='http://www.talkingsupe.com/2012/11/review-all-in-by-raine-miller.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Review posted on Talk Supe</a>
</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"With Ethan everything was fast, intense…combustive."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Before I begin my review, I have to tell you I may be a bit biased when it comes to this book. You see, when I read the first book of this series, Naked, I had envisioned the hero, Ethan Blackstone, to be David Gandy. As some of you may know, I am a bit obsessed with that beautiful man. Okay, maybe not a little – more like a LOT obsessed. So when I read the teaser for ALL IN and realized that it would </span>
  <span id="freeText13617231355172781608" style="display:none"><b>
  <a href="http://www.talkingsupe.com/2012/11/review-all-in-by-raine-miller.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Review posted on Talk Supe</a>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"With Ethan everything was fast, intense…combustive."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Before I begin my review, I have to tell you I may be a bit biased when it comes to this book. You see, when I read the first book of this series, Naked, I had envisioned the hero, Ethan Blackstone, to be David Gandy. As some of you may know, I am a bit obsessed with that beautiful man. Okay, maybe not a little – more like a LOT obsessed. So when I read the teaser for ALL IN and realized that it would be told through Ethan Blackstone’s POV (a.k.a David Gandy’s POV) I was a little more than excited to read this book. Basically, any book that can keep David Gandy running through my mind is a must read. I could barely contain myself waiting for the book to finally show up on release day and nearly had a conniption as I was reading it.<br><br>Naked was a great start but it was fairly short (about 100+ pages) and it had my mouth drooling enough to make me crave for more. In Naked, Brynne and Ethan meet and embark in a passionate affair that neither one had ever experienced. The attraction between the two was instantaneous and once they took their relationship to a physical level, each was equally addicted to the other. Their relationship was fiery hot and it seemed like it would be ending on that note, but then Raine Miller sort of left the reader in a cliffhanger.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I had broken her trust. I'd wagered to high and lost."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>ALL IN picks up right where Naked left off but this time around we are getting the continuation of the story from Ethan’s point of view. Brynne has just found out a secret that he’s kept from her and is utterly devastated. She walks out of his life and tells him to never contact her, again. Brynne had consumed so much of Ethan’s thoughts lately that the thought of not seeing or touching her nearly drives him crazy. He’s in the midst of hatching up a plan to make her take him back when he hears of news about Brynne’s safety. Compelled to keep her safe and out of danger, Ethan barrels his way back into Brynne’s life and leaves her very little room to push him away. Ethan was protective of Brynne from the very beginning but now that Brynne may be in clear and present danger, he's even more protective and possessive over her.<br><br>ALL IN is twice as long as Naked so you get more of a story in this installment. Being inside Ethan head was really interesting and something that I enjoyed. Often times, we only see stories from the females point of view so it's always refreshing to see it from the guys. In Naked, Ethan mainly showed his possessive, bossy and dominate side. We still see all of that in All In but we also get a glimpse at his fears, vulnerability, and dark secrets that he's kept for so many years.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Can I say wicked hormones changing my girl into Medusa and scaring the hell out of me?"<br>"Women…..frightening creatures."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>As much as I enjoyed Ethan's sexy and playful side, I really fell even more madly in love with him because he was just a regular dude. You'd think someone as cool as Ethan wouldn't care about his friends or family liking his woman, but he cares. A lot. I also liked that fact that he could be left baffled about a woman's period as much as any regular Joe on the street. I've read other reviewers say that it seemed like Ethan was a totally different person than what we had originally seen in Naked. My answer to that would be it's because it's what Brynne had portrayed for us. Of course she's going to harp on him being this domineering Alpha male. I liked the fact that Raine Miller gave us Ethan's perspective because too often we're only shown the "cool" side of a man and don't see the whole spectrum. I'm sorry but every man, no matter what age, will always be a little freaked out about his woman being on the rag and ready to bite his head off. Even if he's an ex-Special Forces and top notch security specialist.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I wanted to make love to her....slowly. I could just picture her gorgeous body stretched out naked for me to pleasure in every way I could manage it. All mine. For me alone. Brynne made me feel everything "</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Ethan is still sexy as hell and knows how to please his woman. Raine Miller sure knows how to write some very hot scenes that'll left me fanning myself even when it was probably 50 degrees inside my house. Ethan displayed the depths of his emotions and his need to claim and possess Brynne was intense and scary but at the same time extremely hot. He and Brynne are working through their problems but the amount of effort he's willing to put in is really impeccable. They're relationship will always have ups and downs especially with all the baggage they carry but they are definitely making progress and their bond continues to go deeper with each passing day.<br><br>Overall, All In was very good read that I enjoyed thoroughly and I cannot wait for the final installment to be released later this year. Raine has mentioned that it will mostly likely be released on Dec. 31, so it's starting to look like I will be spending New Years Eve cuddle up on the couch reading the final installment of this addictive series.<br><br>------------------------------<br>November 11, 2012<br><b>4.5 SMEXY STARS!!!</b><br><br><b>Ethan soaking in his tub…</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379795501i/606000._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oooo… I really loved this one and I especially loved being inside that sexy head of Ethan Blackstone. The first book in the Blackstone Affair series, Naked, was good but All In was..…<b>
  <i>HOT DAMN THIS SHIT IS SO GOOD</i>
</b>. <br><br>We got to see the many different facets of Ethan Blackstone, from his confident, cocky, vulnerable and jealous side. I loved hearing everything that went on inside that head of his and discover just how head over heels in love this man was for his beautiful American girl. There is just so much more to Ethan than being a bossy and domineering security specialist. <br><br>Excellent job Ms. Miller!! You definitely have me craving for more of this series and I cannot wait for the next book. <br><br>*Full Review to Come<br><br>One of my favorite Ethan Blackstone quotes:<br><b>
  <i>"I love that fucking wall."</i>
</b> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380391039i/753127.jpg" width="300" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>------------------------------<br><b>YES! CAN.NOT.WAIT.FOR.THIS. <br>Ethan Blackstone is my new boyfriend!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380391039i/753128._SY540_.jpg" width="250" height="340''&gt;" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="13617231355172781608" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer452018109" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6775163614773297666"><br/>Review posted at: <a href='http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Swept Away By Romance</a><br/><br/><b>4 Stars! I was ALL IN...hook, line and sinker! Great second installment, but the ending had me scratching my head!</b> <br/><br/>A pretty good second installment in this series, but not quite as riveting as the first book. Through the first few chapters the reader definitely feels the anguish and desperation that consumes Ethan over the mess he’s in with Brynne. He gives himself a good bashing and is very self-deprecating, not that I felt he needed to be. I loved being i</span>
  <span id="freeText6775163614773297666" style="display:none"><br>Review posted at: <a href="http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Swept Away By Romance</a><br><br><b>4 Stars! I was ALL IN...hook, line and sinker! Great second installment, but the ending had me scratching my head!</b> <br><br>A pretty good second installment in this series, but not quite as riveting as the first book. Through the first few chapters the reader definitely feels the anguish and desperation that consumes Ethan over the mess he’s in with Brynne. He gives himself a good bashing and is very self-deprecating, not that I felt he needed to be. I loved being in Ethan’s head, he’s quite the character and one of the most possessive jealous heroes I’ve ever had the pleasure to read about. His endless mind rambling and slip of the tongue, had me laughing out loud and made him even more appealing, which I didn’t think was possible. <b>No Ethan Blackstone you are NOT a moron, I think you’re pretty damn special!!</b> <br><br>What really tugged at my heart was how he set his pride aside and sought his father out for advice and little parental comfort. What ensued was an unbelievably sweet and emotional scene, which humanized Ethan and showed us his softer side…different from the <b>horn-dog</b> that we’ve grown to love. <br><br> <i>"Lucky us, we can be fucked up together."</i><br><br>While the first book was raw and passionate, this one had a little more of a romantic element. Ethan and Brynne’s relationship becomes clearly defined, and the two of them heat up the sheets…make-up sex that lasted throughout the book…Raine Miller knows her way around passion and sensuality…six ways to Sunday and back! I never felt like it was too much though, and at times the writing was graphic, but when necessary the author leaves us to our imagination, she doesn’t over burden us with description. <br><br>I found I liked Brynne even more than I did in the first book, when she accepts partial blame for the bad that came between her and Ethan. She’s a pretty tough cookie when she needs to be, and what's that big, bad Ethan Blackstone’s, a ring in your nose??<br> <br>We are introduced to a whole host of very interesting secondary characters, that give the book a more personal and family feel. I think love might be in the air for some of them, and if it’s not already, I would love to see Jonathan Blackstone with a certain Aunt Marie! Hint, hint! I also enjoyed the witty banter between Ethan and his cousin, Ivan. Boys will be boys!<br><br>Whether it is a sweet, passionate, humorous, or heartbreaking scene, Raine Miller skillfully masters all of them with exceptional writing. Even during the scenes that just depicted daily life, I was glued to the book. However, I wanted a little more meat to the story in the way of the suspense and danger that’s been hinted at towards Brynne, and the ending left me…suspended…like something was missing. I didn’t get that final bite, as if someone took the last morsel of food off my plate…THAT feeling! I’m not even going to go into the epilogue…hence me scratching my head…that’s all I’m going to say and these are the reasons for the 4 star rating. <br><br>Still and all, worth the wait, I’m hooked on this series, this author writing, and I’m hoping that whatever was missing here, we’ll find it in the next book. I have no doubt that Raine Miller will deliver.<br><br><b>My stressed out Ethan is having trouble kicking the habit! Poor baby…I would love to keep his mouth occupied with other things! *snicker snort*</b> <br><a href="http://s1130.beta.photobucket.com/user/kparks823/library/David%20Gandy" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397048i/765828._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>Ethan’s song <i>My Girl</i> by the Temptations...we know she's yours!!</b><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=bZh7nRw6gl8">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=bZh7nR...</a><br></span>

<div id="review_420208947" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Brandy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4995048-brandy"><img alt="Brandy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1494288181p2/4995048.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/420208947?book_show_action=true">Sep 22, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brandy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brandy" href="/user/show/4995048-brandy">Brandy</a>
      </span>

        rated it

<span id="freeTextContainer13508898884008988659">Book review 11/9/12: Awesome book 2... Highly entertaining throughout most of it. My only complaint is that it seemed to drag at times, where as book one kept my interest throughout the whole thing & had me begging for more at the end. Not that I wanted another cliffhanger because hell no I absolutely did not. lol. Don't get me wrong, I still loved the book, slight dragging & all. Who wouldn't love Ethan & all of his yummy glory?   <span id="freeText13508898884008988659" style="display:none">Book review 11/9/12: Awesome book 2... Highly entertaining throughout most of it. My only complaint is that it seemed to drag at times, where as book one kept my interest throughout the whole thing &amp; had me begging for more at the end. Not that I wanted another cliffhanger because hell no I absolutely did not. lol. Don't get me wrong, I still loved the book, slight dragging &amp; all. Who wouldn't love Ethan &amp; all of his yummy glory? He is probably one of my favorite male characters &amp; I just loved that this book was written from his PoV. We really got a glimpse into his heart &amp; mind &amp; what a fantastic heart &amp; mind it is! BTW - Anyone who hasn't read this book yet, will be glad to know that there is no horrible, I'm-going-to-ruin-your-life-until-the-next-book-comes-out cliffhanger at the end. lol That was very refreshing &amp; relieving. **sighs** Needless to say, I didn't do too well with the one in book 1, but I'm all better now. Definitely a series I would recommend &amp; one I will continue to read.<br /><br />Pre-book release comments: <br />Ok... We're at the end of September... The book is supposed to be released next month... I have now stopped hyperventilating. I think I can wait until then, although it will be painfully! Man what a cliffhanger in the last book! Miller really outdid herself! <br /><br />10/7/12... If Miller's website is still correct, the book will hopefully be released at the end of this month... I read this book weeks ago &amp; I am still extremely excited about this book. Usually, I'm over it by now. I think I have to read Naked again, just to get my fix............ lol.<br /><br />10/21/12... I just checked Miller's website again &amp; there is still not a release date, so there is a chance that it will not come out this month either. However, she has said that this one will be a bit longer, so can I really be mad at her for giving us a longer book 2 &amp; it will be from Ethan's POV? Hell no! I hope it won't be too much longer, though... The anticipation is killing me &amp; everyone else, so it seems from everyone else's posts as well. I'm just glad I'm not alone in this &amp; there are others who fill my pain... lol.<br /></span>

<div id="review_449077276" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/449077276" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/449077276?book_show_action=true">Nov 05, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer449077276" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16836052507187157012"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396597i/764672.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396597ra/764673.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> Ok. I loved this book. And I love Ethan Blackstone. A lot. </b><br/><br/>This is a spoiler-free review. <br/><br/>ALL IN starts off exactly the moment after book #1, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15852756.Naked__The_Blackstone_Affair___1_' title='Naked (The Blackstone Affair, #1) by Raine Miller' rel='nofollow noopener'>Naked</a>, ends and continues the story from Ethan’s point of view.<br/><br/>As a quick recap/intro, Ethan is the head of a high end security firm hired to protect Brynne, an American student studying in London. When they meet, they have an undeniable connection and so begins their story…<br/><br/><blockquote> <i> “She was different from the beginning. Special. My beautiful American girl…. it </i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText16836052507187157012" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396597i/764672.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396597ra/764673.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> Ok. I loved this book. And I love Ethan Blackstone. A lot. </b><br><br>This is a spoiler-free review. <br><br>ALL IN starts off exactly the moment after book #1, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15852756.Naked__The_Blackstone_Affair___1_" title="Naked (The Blackstone Affair, #1) by Raine Miller" rel="nofollow noopener">Naked</a>, ends and continues the story from Ethan’s point of view.<br><br>As a quick recap/intro, Ethan is the head of a high end security firm hired to protect Brynne, an American student studying in London. When they meet, they have an undeniable connection and so begins their story…<br><br><blockquote> <i> “She was different from the beginning. Special. My beautiful American girl…. it became so much more for me than just a job.” </i>
</blockquote>  <br><br>All In is a sexy, fast-paced story of two flawed but functional characters… If you’re looking for a book with a possessive, protective and swoon-worthy Alpha hero, this series will deliver.<br><br>Raine Miller just nailed Ethan’s voice. Unlike book #1, this entire book is told from Ethan’s perspective and I just couldn’t get enough of it! I guess I felt that after reading Naked I had a pretty good handle on what was going on inside Brynne’s mind, but getting inside Ethan’s head really helped round out the story. Everything about it just made me either laugh or swoon – his jealousies, how crazy in love with her he was, his protective instincts (and the reason behind them)… all of it was just so addictive and we really got to see all sides of his character! haha, not to mention the hilarious part about him dealing with a PMSing girlfriend:<br><br><blockquote> <i> “Then I drove over to get my snake-haired, sharp-tongued, unpredictable, and very perplexing girlfriend, like the besotted sap that I very much was.<br>Women… frightening creatures.” </i>
</blockquote>  <br>One thing I love about Ethan is that he has no problem admitting that he fucked up. It takes a real man to do that and I appreciated the raw honesty it gave the story where when mistakes were made, the characters would admit to them and then try to move on functionally. And I loved that Brynne was understanding about it all too. She certainly had good reason to be upset at times but she came around in a timely fashion that made me feel sympathetic and understanding towards her. I also felt like all the mistakes that were made in this book were certainly forgivable ones. No stupidity here! It was refreshing and welcome to not have to deal with any frustrating character traits.<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> “I was drawn to you from the first moment I saw your portrait. I had to know you. And then to be with you. To have you look at me and really see me. I know now that I fell in love. I fell in love with a beautiful American girl. You, Brynne.<br><br>… And even if you hate me for what I did, I’ll still love you. If you won’t see me, I’ll still love you. I’ll still love you because you are mine. Mine, Brynne. In my heart you are, and nobody can take that away from me. Not even you.” </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br>That being said, neither Ethan nor Brynne were “perfect” characters. They certainly had their ups and downs and they were both flawed, but in a way that made you want to know more about them and sympathize with what they were going through.<br><br>In this book, we learn more about both Ethan and Brynne’s rather painful back stories and get to understand what haunts their dreams.<br><br><blockquote> <i> “You have your dark place and I have mine. I understand.” </i>
</blockquote>  <br>It was really wonderful to read about a couple who supported each other through their problems and both genuinely wanted to just make things work.<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> “If you come with me you’re signing on for all of me, Brynne. I don’t know any other way to be with you. It’s all in for me. And I want it to be all in for you too.” </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br>I seriously can’t get enough of Ethan’s POV. He was just so adorably Alpha. I read just smiling to myself at seeing him be all growly and protective of her. Totally endearing!<br><br>I’m not sure why but before I started, I kind of thought this was a BDSM series. Not a clue what gave me that idea but for record, it’s not. That said, it’s still hot, steamy and erotic. Possessive Alpha male hero, remember? <br><br>This was one of those books where the pages flew by. It’s longer than the first one, but at about 250 pages it’s still a quick, fast-paced read.<br><br>The story kind of just ends, but thankfully, there was no relationship cliffhanger. There are still bad guys out there who need to be caught and a whole mess of things to sort out, but at least we are left off with them strong as a couple. **whew**<br><br>I can’t wait for book #3. I’ll be devouring it the moment it gets released on May 14, 2013.<br><br>4.5 stars<br><br>And... since David Gandy was the inspiration for Ethan Blackstone.... here are a whole bunch of casting images (and gif above) :)<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396597i/764674.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396597i/764675.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389730i/751025.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="16836052507187157012" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer484197628" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15683578016265695174"><a href='http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/MillerAllin2TitlebySueBee_zps833ab7a7.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401847i/780479.jpg' alt=' photo MillerAllin2TitlebySueBee_zps833ab7a7.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a href='http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20heroine/kpBubysb_zps6598f11e.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><b>★★★★★! All in, book 2 of 4. The suspenseful continuation of Ethan Blackstone’s all-consuming romance saga with his American girl while trying to protect her & uncover secrets in a deadly high-stakes political game!</b><br/><br/><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“It’s all in for me. And I want it to be all in for you too.” <br/>“All in?” She brought her palm to my cheek and held it there, her questioning look so genuine…<br/>…“A poker term. Means to bet everything you have on the cards you’re holding. You’re what I’m holding.”</b>
   </i></blockquote></a></span>
  <span id="freeText15683578016265695174" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/MillerAllin2TitlebySueBee_zps833ab7a7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401847i/780479.jpg" alt=" photo MillerAllin2TitlebySueBee_zps833ab7a7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20heroine/kpBubysb_zps6598f11e.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392520412ra/8572767.gif" alt=" photo kpBubysb_zps6598f11e.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>★★★★★! All in, book 2 of 4. The suspenseful continuation of Ethan Blackstone’s all-consuming romance saga with his American girl while trying to protect her &amp; uncover secrets in a deadly high-stakes political game!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“It’s all in for me. And I want it to be all in for you too.” <br>“All in?” She brought her palm to my cheek and held it there, her questioning look so genuine…<br>…“A poker term. Means to bet everything you have on the cards you’re holding. You’re what I’m holding.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>The spectacular <b>Blackstone Affair series</b> follows world-renowned security expert and owner of Blackstone International Ltd., Ethan Blackstone in his whirlwind romance with American born University of London student Brynne Bennett. When Brynne’s past comes back to haunt her, Ethan sets out to protect and solve the mystery of a treacherous and deadly high stake political game involving the Vice Presidency for the United States. No one is safe, and neither is the heart of sworn playboy Ethan. One look at Brynne and he is determined to have her at any cost!<br><br><u>SOMERSET HISTORICALS</u><br><b>Book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/487216719" rel="nofollow noopener">The Passion of Darius</a></b><br><i>Darius &amp; Marianne (year 1837)</i><br><b>Book 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/484467328" rel="nofollow noopener">The Undoing of a Libertine</a></b><br><i>Jeremy &amp; Georgina (year 1837)</i><br><br><u>THE BLACKSTONE AFFAIR</u> - Ethan &amp; Brynne<br><b>Book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/484197621" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Naked</a><br>Book 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/484197628" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">All In</a><br>Book 3: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/486089526" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Eyes Wide Open</a><br>Book 4: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/616673715" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Rare and Precious Things</a><br>Book 5: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2201351790" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">The Blessings of Ethan Blackstone</a></b><br><br><b>All In (book 2) opens upright after chocking cliffhanger ending of book 1.</b> Both Ethan and Brynne have taken a nose-dive and while they both try to find their way through the storm the plot thickens yet again. This is Ethan’s story – watch as he comes back with a vengeance set on making everything right.<br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/MillerAllin2HerobySueBee_zpsf2b25a5a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401847i/780480.jpg" alt=" photo MillerAllin2HerobySueBee_zpsf2b25a5a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>All In is told entirely from <b>Ethan Blackstone’s POV</b>. And what a privilege and joy it is to get a glimpse into the enigma that is Ethan. <br><br>Women had always come easy for the extraordinary Ethan. Brief affairs conducted at his f~ck-pad adjacent to his office is how the elusive playboy whored his way through life. That is until Brynne. Seeing that photograph of Brynne, his American girl, put Ethan’s life in a tail-spin. <br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I couldn’t remember ever being driven by my c~ck in the way I was driven with her. Maybe when I was just starting out, but nothing with this level of intensity had ever consumed me like it did now. F~cking Brynne was right up there with food, and shelter these days.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><b>Brynne was his game-changer!</b> Bet all – All in. He will never be the same.<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“…rendering me utterly captive and raging to claim her body with the dominating sex I couldn’t seem to control when we were together. My ultimate reward and my greatest fear all rolled into one.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>Six words to describe Ethan: <b>Unforgettable, dominant, enigmatic, smart, captivating and driven.</b> <br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/MillerAllin2HeroinebySueBee_zps6e4d2a52.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401847i/780481.jpg" alt=" photo MillerAllin2HeroinebySueBee_zps6e4d2a52.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Brynne Bennett</b> is finding her footing and coming to terms with her feelings for Ethan while learning how to exist next to the intense, dominant, assured, yet possessive Ethan. <br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I felt like Ethan wanted to consume me at times. He overwhelmed me from the first and was definitely a demanding lover, but one thing was certain, I wanted everything he’d ever given me.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>What she has yet to see is that though she may have no control in the threats and danger she is facing, she is the one with all the control when it comes to Ethan and their relationship. Rarely have I seen such a whopped man.<br><br>Five words to describe Brynne: <b>Tenuous, determined, fragile, enchanting and compelling.</b><br><br>Though book 2 does not have a huge cliff-hanger ending it leads right to book 3, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/486089526" rel="nofollow noopener">Eyes Wide Open</a>. <b>Addictive and suspenseful plot!. Spellbinding storytelling! Unforgettable Ethan! A must-read series! Thanks again Ms. Miller!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“When I reached for my girl and showed her how much I did indeed need her, and told her with words too, I knew then that the best gamble of my life had not been the cards I’d played, but that one night on a London street, when a beautiful American girl tried to walk out in the dark, and I played the most important hand I’d ever been dealt, and went… all in.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>

  <span id="freeText2611452515305991219" style="display:none">I was super duper excited when this got released.         <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer453439980" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16732184585017085106">I loved book one but this one read as if someone else wrote it. Ethan is portrayed in such a juvenile fashion, I was hard pressed to remember that man is in his 30's. All the hard, rough, charismatic edginess that I loved in Ethan in book one is replaced by a simpering, hormonal teenager. Paired with a weak story line, annoyingly crude dialogue, and it's one dimensional presentation, I am floored by how different this book is written. </span>

          </span>

<div id="review_427330305" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/427330305" />
    <a title="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8524618-angie---angie-s-dreamy-reads"><img alt="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1578074503p2/8524618.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/427330305?book_show_action=true">Oct 03, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" href="/user/show/8524618-angie---angie-s-dreamy-reads">Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer427330305" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12382920966973325587"><b>3.5 SEXY ETHAN STARS</b><br/><br/>I was really excited to read the highly anticipated sequel to Raine Millers first book Naked. So on release day I immediately put down what I was reading to pick it up. There were a couple things that I didn't like and I want to get them out of the way so I can <b>GUSH</b> about the things I did <b>LOVE.</b> All In was good but left me thinking and feeling a little differently than the first book. In the first book "Naked" you were left on the edge of your seat screaming at your kindle <b>"NO</b></span>
  <span id="freeText12382920966973325587" style="display:none"><b>3.5 SEXY ETHAN STARS</b><br><br>I was really excited to read the highly anticipated sequel to Raine Millers first book Naked. So on release day I immediately put down what I was reading to pick it up. There were a couple things that I didn't like and I want to get them out of the way so I can <b>GUSH</b> about the things I did <b>LOVE.</b> All In was good but left me thinking and feeling a little differently than the first book. In the first book "Naked" you were left on the edge of your seat screaming at your kindle <b>"NO, NO, NO, it can't be over!!!"</b> but with All In I lacked those feelings!!!! I felt like Ethan lost a lot of the alpha male qualities that I loved so much about him in the first book and I also felt like the story lacked any action or suspense. I really didn't feel like I was sitting on the edge of my seat waiting to find out what was going to happen, which in the first book I definitely was. Those are a couple of the things I didn't love <b>
  <u>BUT</u>
</b> there were also plenty of things that I did love. I loved the way Ethan took care of Brynne. I liked hearing how deep his feelings ran for her and how much he craved and needed her in his life. I loved the chemistry which is never lacking and I absolutely <b>ADORED</b> Ethan's dirty mouth. I think Ethan showed a softer side in this book which was admirable and I also enjoyed the fact that he was jealous and possessive over Brynne.<br><br><br>All In picks up right where we left off with Ethan at the elevator chasing after Brynne who has just found out that Ethan lied to her about something that was a pivotal moment in Brynne's life. Ethan struggles to comes to grips with the idea that Brynne has left him and decides that there is <i>NO WAY</i> he is going to give up on her.<br><br><b><i>"Never</i> is a very long time. I might be able to give her a day or two, but never was irrefutably out of the question." ~~ Ethan</b><br><br>With this revelation Ethan decides to write Brynne a letter letting her know why he made the choice to lie by omission. Once receiving the letter Brynne decides to call Ethan because she's scared and missing him. With that phone call Ethan rushes out to meet Brynne and things are completely different between them. Ethan is hundred percent in love with Brynne and let's Brynne know that he is <b>NEVER</b> going to let her go and that in this relationship he is All In and there is no chance of her running away from him. <br><br><b>"I am. With you, Brynne, I am, and I have been from the very start."<br>And I meant every word. I know what I wanted. I understood it crystal clear and there was no turning back with her now. <i>All in is forever, baby...</i></b><br><br>Ethan and Brynne are both struggling with demons from their past which were sort of addressed. Ethan's demons come a bit more to the forefront of the book and we see Ethan struggle to open up to Brynne and let her into his deepest and darkest side.<br><br>Ethan has a serious addiction to Brynne (and Djarum's). He feels the need to claim her and mark her and possess her <b>ALL OF THE TIME</b>. The sex in this book is extremely hot and Ethan's dirty mouth is incredible. I love their sexual connection which I felt went to so much deeper than just hot f*cking. They were completely sexually compatible and in love with each other, which made me melt.<br><br><b>"I wanted to make love to her....slowly. I could just picture her gorgeous body stretched out naked for me to pleasure in every way I could manage it. <i> All mine.</i> For me alone. Brynne made me feel everything -" ~~ Ethan</b><br><br>This book leaves you with some answers but also a WHOLE lot more questions which is good because there will be a book 3 in the series. I'm excited to continue to read about Ethan and Brynne and find out what awaits them in the future. I have a feeling that something BIG is going to happen because the ending in All In left me with a funny inkling that things are about to turn interesting. Overall I thought it was a good addition to the series but I had hoped for a little more.<br><br><br><u>Favorite quote in the book ~~</u><br><i>
  <b>"...the best gamble of my life had not been the cards I'd been played, but that one night on a London street, when a beautiful American girl tried to walk in the dark, and I played the most important hand I'd ever dealt, and went...all in." ~~ Ethan </b>
</i><br><br>Ethan &lt;3<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380746966i/3118747.jpg" width="369" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Ethan and Brynne &lt;3<br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380391053i/753136.jpg" width="500" height="332" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="12382920966973325587" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <i>hit it off by talking books- something trending about a very young billionaire and his obsession with an even younger woman... and sex... </b> <br><br>I was so excited about this book.. Couldn't wait for it! It was worth it. <br><br><u>The Story...</u> <br><br>Thankfully it picks up right where it left us. At the elevator. <br><br>Ethan knows that he lied to Brynne but is not going to give up. <br><br><b>
  <i>Never was a long time. I might be able to give her a day or two, but never was was irrefutably out of the question.</i>
</b><br><br>He has to be with her more than he needs to breathe, and he has to know she's safe. <br><br>The threat to Brynne still lurks and the Olympics are gaining on Ethan's company. <br><br>This second installment covers their relationship turning into exactly that. A relationship. There is still a lot of sex but also feelings, talking etc like normal people. <br>Sharing their secrets with each other. <br><br><u>Thoughts </u> <br><br>This started off with a bang! <span id="freeTextContainer14192067589315171357"> <b>5 stars for the one and only <br/> **HOT/SEXY Mr.Blackstone**</b> <br/><br/> <b>"I want my cock in you all night long."</b><br/><br/><br/><i>This is the continued love story of Ethan and Brynne. It picks right up where "NAKED" ended. "ALL IN" is told in Ethan's POV, and he is just PERFECT and AMAZING. Ethan has some secrets in his past, that have not been revealed and we are just now seeing the whole truth about poor Brynne's past.               <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer436236648" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10858339627143019770">After the ending of <i>Naked</i>, things are not going very well for Ethan and Brynne. They both have a lot of baggage not to mention the new threat that is hanging over Brynne's head. They really need to find a way to <i>trust</i> each other. <br/><br/>I loved the emotional drama that the book started off with but again, it was way too short. These two are so passionate that I wanted to <i>feel</i> that. Not just have things swept over. The letter was a nice touch though. And it was interesting getting the whole book from Et</span>
  <span id="freeText10858339627143019770" style="display:none">After the ending of <i>Naked</i>, things are not going very well for Ethan and Brynne. They both have a lot of baggage not to mention the new threat that is hanging over Brynne's head. They really need to find a way to <i>trust</i> each other. <br><br>I loved the emotional drama that the book started off with but again, it was way too short. These two are so passionate that I wanted to <i>feel</i> that. Not just have things swept over. The letter was a nice touch though. And it was interesting getting the whole book from Ethan's POV...still not sure if it was too much though. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441500909ra/16116500.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, two things that are bothering me...one, I really don't care about the person(s) stalking Brynne. It's boring and Ethan suppose to be this big, hot shot security guy, well, let's see some security magic! And secondly, the sex...I know this is going to sound horrible but it's gotten old. Even though they are doing different things, it just sounds rehashed and I was feeling a mighty need to skim! <br><br>However, I did really like the rest of it. I still love Ethan's vulnerability and he's just too sweet! It was wonderful how he takes care of Brynne and how he took care of business with her mom and dad. I also liked that they are both opening up to each other. <br><br>Things get stepped up at the end with lots of drama and Ethan and Brynne taking off for his sister's house. I have a feeling things are going to take an interesting albeit predictable turn in the next book, <i>Eyes Wide Open</i>.<br><br>♦ Don't miss the cute story from Simba's POV at the end!<br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438836063i/15761015.jpg" width="400" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quote:</u>
</b><br><br>♥ <i>"And even if you hate me for what I did, I’ll still love you. If you won’t see me, I’ll still love you. I’ll still love you because you are mine. Mine, Brynne. In my heart you are, and nobody can take that away from me. Not even you. <br> E "</i></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3194546-crista?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3194546-crista?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3194546-crista?shelf=tortured-heroes">tortured-heroes</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer454768261" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer244350827958398391">Very Disappointing!<br/><br/>After being so excited, mesmerized, and blown away by <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15852756.Naked__The_Blackstone_Affair___1_' title='Naked (The Blackstone Affair, #1) by Raine Miller' rel='nofollow noopener'>Naked</a>, I couldn't wait to start the second book of the Blackstone trilogy. What a bummer it turned out to be.<br/><br/>Ethan was just about my perfect hero in Naked. He was confident, successful, caring, considerate, and completely fixated and obsessed with Brynne. I was expecting my love and obsession for this character to intensify with this second installment, and instead I am left feeling like I just had a bucket of cold water du</span>
  <span id="freeText244350827958398391" style="display:none">Very Disappointing!<br /><br />After being so excited, mesmerized, and blown away by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15852756.Naked__The_Blackstone_Affair___1_" title="Naked (The Blackstone Affair, #1) by Raine Miller" rel="nofollow noopener">Naked</a>, I couldn't wait to start the second book of the Blackstone trilogy. What a bummer it turned out to be.<br /><br />Ethan was just about my perfect hero in Naked. He was confident, successful, caring, considerate, and completely fixated and obsessed with Brynne. I was expecting my love and obsession for this character to intensify with this second installment, and instead I am left feeling like I just had a bucket of cold water dumped over my head! What had me so "hot and bothered" in the first book has left me "cold and disinterested" in the second.<br /><br />All In is told from Ethan's POV. Usually this change in view point would excite me, and it did....at first. Then all of a sudden, Ethan started coming across whiny, insecure, and immature. His "voice", for lack of a better term, seemed completely contrary to the man I fell so hard for in book 1. There were too many times where I felt that Ethan's thoughts and feeling seemed completely out of character...not only for his character, but for men in general. I could tell that the author was a woman who was trying to write from a man's perspective and that kept pulling me out of the story. If a story is going to be told from a man's POV, I have to believe it's what a man would be thinking,feeling, or saying. That never happened with this book.<br /><br />Another issue I had was with the plot. There really was none. I'm all for sex, but this book lacked much else, and the bummer is that there were so many potential plot lines that could've been explored.<br /><br />Bummer. Not sure I will even finish this trilogy, but with all this being said...<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15852756.Naked__The_Blackstone_Affair___1_" title="Naked (The Blackstone Affair, #1) by Raine Miller" rel="nofollow noopener">Naked</a> was brilliant.</span>
  <a data-text-id="244350827958398391" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer4725467887220335119">5 Dirty Talking Stars!!!!!!<br/><br/><a href='http://www.imagechef.com/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380412925i/812352.jpg' alt='ImageChef.com - Get codes for Facebook, Hi5, MySpace and more' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> </a><br/><br/><i>All In</i> is the continuation of Brynne and Ethan's love affair ♥ Ethan has broken Brynne's trust; she trusted him with her heart and to always tell her the truth, but he failed and now he has to win her back.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>“I wouldn’t ever keep the truth from her again.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>We learn much more about Brynne's shocking past, how she feels about it and how they deal with it as a couple. <br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Ethan knows what happened to me and there is no way he could possibly love me now.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><a title='By Lies Thru a Lens  (Gemma Uploaded by tm) [CC-BY-2.0 (http://creativecommons.org/licenses/by/2.0)], via Wikimedia Commons' href='http://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/File%3AGemma_(8447283481).jpg' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img width='256' alt='Gemma (8447283481)' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380746968i/3118748.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/>♥ </span>
  <span id="freeText4725467887220335119" style="display:none">5 Dirty Talking Stars!!!!!!<br><br><a href="http://www.imagechef.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380412925i/812352.jpg" alt="ImageChef.com - Get codes for Facebook, Hi5, MySpace and more" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a><br><br><i>All In</i> is the continuation of Brynne and Ethan's love affair ♥ Ethan has broken Brynne's trust; she trusted him with her heart and to always tell her the truth, but he failed and now he has to win her back.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I wouldn’t ever keep the truth from her again.”</i>
</b><br><br>We learn much more about Brynne's shocking past, how she feels about it and how they deal with it as a couple. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Ethan knows what happened to me and there is no way he could possibly love me now.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><a title="By Lies Thru a Lens  (Gemma Uploaded by tm) [CC-BY-2.0 (http://creativecommons.org/licenses/by/2.0)], via Wikimedia Commons" href="http://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/File%3AGemma_(8447283481).jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <b>
    <i>“I know now that I fell in love. I fell in love with a beautiful American girl. You, Brynne.”</i>

</blockquote><br><br><a href="http://www.imagechef.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380746968i/3118749.jpg" alt="ImageChef.com - Get codes for Facebook, Hi5, MySpace and more" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a><br>♥ ♥ ♥<br><br>The story is told from Ethan’s POV which I found utterly delightful. I thoroughly enjoyed his dirty talking mouth and romantic ways. He is delicious in every way and when Brynne and Ethan get together the sparks fly and it is HOT, HOT, HOT!!!!<br><br><b>

She flowed in a rhythm with me.”<br><br>“I’m going to make you come so hard, and you’re going to think of nothing but me when I do.”<br><br>“Making you come under my tongue is the sexiest thing in the world. How you move. How you taste. How you sound when you get there…” <br>♥<br><br>Brynne still needs protecting from a threat that could prove to be extremely dangerous and Ethan will do whatever it takes to keep her safe.<br><blockquote>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer539050251" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer12009847631437332402">So I liked it...hence the three stars. It passed the time. But I wasn't bowled over. There was a LOT of obsession on Ethan's end. Every single thought was about Brynne. It was worse than reading a YA book with loads of hard ons. Seriously, the man gets a hard on every time he thinks of Brynne...which is ALL THE TIME!<br/><br/>However, I tend to like the super protective men, and Ethan is definitely that, or at least tries to be. Not Kristen Ashley protective by any means...the man runs a security firm but</span>
  <span id="freeText12009847631437332402" style="display:none">So I liked it...hence the three stars. It passed the time. But I wasn't bowled over. There was a LOT of obsession on Ethan's end. Every single thought was about Brynne. It was worse than reading a YA book with loads of hard ons. Seriously, the man gets a hard on every time he thinks of Brynne...which is ALL THE TIME!<br /><br />However, I tend to like the super protective men, and Ethan is definitely that, or at least tries to be. Not Kristen Ashley protective by any means...the man runs a security firm but "lost" Brynne three times during the course of this book! That's a lot of losing! But he sure does pitch a great man fit when she's gone. I just love when a man grovels and chases.<br /><br />I know I'm getting somewhat stingy with my stars :( I think the big allure about this series was the naked picture obsession, how Ethan fell in lust/love with Brynne just from seeing her picture, and then proceeds to nail down the object of his desire. That's a fantasy inducing plot right there. Brynne girl has it really going on, and she leads our man on a merry little (really little) chase. But now that this intriguing fiasco is over, what's left? <br /><br />The "new" in this book is that Brynne and Ethan's pasts are revealed in a big way, and each are pretty horrifying in their own right. I had no idea that it would be quite so bad. The empathy factor sure got amped up. And Brynne's past is coming for her...the question is how Ethan will manage to protect and save her, all while convincing her to let the past lie. She needs to heal and move on, and he's helping her just by accepting her.<br /><br /></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/447436823?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

<span id="freeTextContainer7182505058224978134"><b>PGJ's (Pavlina & Georgia & JenRider) Weekend BookClub!</b><br/><br/>"All in" according to <i>Wikipedia</i><br/>A player faced with a current bet who wishes to call but has insufficient remaining stake, may bet the remainder of his stake and declare himself all in. <br/><br/>"All in" according to (the one and only) <i>Ethan Blackstone</i><br/>If you come with me you’re signing on for all of me, Brynne. I don’t know any other way to be with you. It’s all in for me. And I want it to be all in for you too. [...] A poker term. Means to bet everyth</span>
  <span id="freeText7182505058224978134" style="display:none"><b>PGJ's (Pavlina &amp; Georgia &amp; JenRider) Weekend BookClub!</b><br><br>"All in" according to <i>Wikipedia</i><br>A player faced with a current bet who wishes to call but has insufficient remaining stake, may bet the remainder of his stake and declare himself all in. <br><br>"All in" according to (the one and only) <i>Ethan Blackstone</i><br>If you come with me you’re signing on for all of me, Brynne. I don’t know any other way to be with you. It’s all in for me. And I want it to be all in for you too. [...] A poker term. Means to bet everything you have on the cards you’re holding. You’re what I’m holding.<br><br>OH MY ETHAN...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396344ra/763860.gif" width="176" height="197" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My Rating: Another clear night sky for this book!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380391945i/754655._SX540_.jpg" width="300" height="225" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>MILLION STARS!<br><br>I won't bother with a blurp, because if you read the first book (and most of you certainly did), y'all know that this book picks up immediately where the other one left us but (a huge BUT) be prepared ladies because we are in the mind of Ethan Blackstone!!!<br><br>The entire book is from Ethan's point of view and I found it refreshing and highly entertaining. Not many authors are brave enough to sell us a romance (and a break-up in particular) from a guy's perspective but when you work with Ethan Blackstone you can't lose.<br><br><i>
  <b>I have demons too.I am terrified of facing them without you.I don’t know what I’m doing most of the time but I do know how I feel about you.And even if you hate me for what I did, I’ll still love you.If you won’t see me,I’ll still love you.I’ll still love you because you are mine.Mine,Brynne.In my heart you are,and nobody can take that away from me.Not even you.<br><br>You’re not meant to be alone. You’re meant to be with me.</b>
</i><br><br>Ethan is everything I hoped for and the very short 1st book teased us with... Adorable, romantic, funny, witty, sarcastic, dangerous, possesive, obsessive, jealous, FREAKING PERFECT!<br><br>In this book we learn the nature and real story of Brynne's abuse.. The word heartbreaking isn't enough to describe the horrific event.<br>I was stunned and left screaming:<br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380315268ra/689004.gif" width="160" height="89" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But despite the very serious abuse and the warnings about imminent danger, the threat on Brynne seemed a little vague and I expected a little more action but that's a really small flaw for me when there is so much of Ethan and...<br><br>...we have a <b>Best Curse Nomination: “I don’t give a maiden queen’s first fuck what that cocksucker thinks. What is he to you anyway?”</b> I LOVE HIM!!!<br><br>I know all of you naughty girls are gonna fill my homepage with pics like this:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396344i/763861.jpg" width="400" height="664" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm gonna make the difference and post another hot-blooded (more on the cold side) male:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396344i/763862._SX540_.jpg" width="600" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>HELLO SIMBA!! <i> I demand a Nalla for Simba, NOW!!</i><br><br>The glimpse on Ivan and Gabrielle was great and I'm very intrigued about their story when Ethan and Brynne's ends.<br><br><b>December looks months away!! (more like a month, but I enjoy being overly dramatic) and I really think Brynne has somethig wonderful to share with us.<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I'm thinking... pregnancy?!?!?!? Anyone else with me? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> She deserves the spotlight again!</b><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_423639801" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/423639801" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/423639801?book_show_action=true">Sep 28, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer423639801" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18443839896330073882"><b>
  <i>”I don’t know any other way to be with you. It’s all in for me. And I want it to be all in for you too.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>Ethan Blackstone has it BAD for Brynne. His feelings borderline obsession or addiction. He loves her from the get go and those feelings have only intensified with time. His love for Brynne and his desire to keep her safe are put to the test in this sequel.<br/><br/>Brynne finds herself in danger in this sequel:<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392650ra/755883.gif' width='300' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>There is a video somewhere out there documenting a horrific criminal act perpetrated again</span>
  <span id="freeText18443839896330073882" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>”I don’t know any other way to be with you. It’s all in for me. And I want it to be all in for you too.”</i>
</b><br><br>Ethan Blackstone has it BAD for Brynne. His feelings borderline obsession or addiction. He loves her from the get go and those feelings have only intensified with time. His love for Brynne and his desire to keep her safe are put to the test in this sequel.<br><br>Brynne finds herself in danger in this sequel:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392650ra/755883.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There is a video somewhere out there documenting a horrific criminal act perpetrated against her from her past. Ethan is a security specialist and has taken on the job of keeping her safe although I’m still fuzzy as to why she is in danger. She was a victim maybe to keep her quiet as if after all these years she would want to publicize this heinous act?<br><br>If you are looking for closure in All In you will not find it. There are some answers but mostly more questions. This book ends in a cliffhanger just like its predecessor. I will certainly read the next installment to see what and who is threatening Brynne. <br><br></span>
