<div id="review_466797005" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/466797005" />
    <a title="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14351108-deanna-pink-lady"><img alt="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1370640721p2/14351108.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/466797005?book_show_action=true">Nov 30, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" href="/user/show/14351108-deanna-pink-lady">Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14351108-deanna-pink-lady?shelf=hot-and-sexy">hot-and-sexy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14351108-deanna-pink-lady?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer466797005" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer452043243264155541"><u>5 Fabulous ReRead Stars</u>♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥<br/><br/>All In begins where Naked ends. Ethan knows a secret about Brynne and is not forthcoming. She finds out and runs.<br/><br/><b>Ethan knows what happened to me and these is no way he could possible love me now.<br/><br/>I felt like Ethan wanted to consume me at times. He overwhelmed me from the first and was definitely a demanding lover, but one thing was certain, I wanted everything he'd ever given me. I found that out once I left him.</b><br/><br/>Ethan is devastated that Brynne has left but he knows</span>
  <span id="freeText452043243264155541" style="display:none"><u>5 Fabulous ReRead Stars</u>♥ ♥ ♥ ♥ ♥<br><br>All In begins where Naked ends. Ethan knows a secret about Brynne and is not forthcoming. She finds out and runs.<br><br><b>Ethan knows what happened to me and these is no way he could possible love me now.<br><br>I felt like Ethan wanted to consume me at times. He overwhelmed me from the first and was definitely a demanding lover, but one thing was certain, I wanted everything he'd ever given me. I found that out once I left him.</b><br><br>Ethan is devastated that Brynne has left but he knows what he wants and that is Brynne. He will win her back. Failure is not an option. He writes Brynne a letter putting it all out there.<br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/image_zpsb8a8046e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br>Brynne knows that Ethan will keep her safe from the dangers that may await her. But he must earn her trust again, no secrets. So their passionate, hot, steamy, love story continues. <br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/image_zps4e118f2d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br><b>"If you come with me you're signing on for all of me Brynne. I don't know any other way to be with you. It's all in for me. And I want it to be all in for you too." <br>"All in?"<br>"A poker term. Means to bet everything you have on the cards you're holding. You're what I'm holding."</b><br><br>All In takes us in to Ethan and Brynne's relationship. It gives us insight to who they are and what their demons are. Ethan is totally consumed by Brynne and I loved his passion. The whole book is narrated from his perspective and its fabulous. It's great to get in his head.<br><br><b>You are so strong...and lovely...and brilliant, Brynne Bennett. My beautiful American girl.<br><br>Making Brynne want me was my obsession.</b> Gotta love his honesty.<br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/image_zpsdb6446f1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br><b>Brynne was the girl. My girl.<br><br>I didn't want slow with Brynne. I wanted fast and intense and all the time.<br><br>Sex with her shattered me down to my deepest levels of complexity.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/image_zpse6d6469d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br>Did I mention that there is a lot of shagging in this book! Incredibly hot, steamy shagging!! I think I can say that Brynne is a very lucky girl. But what I do see is that Ethan and Brynne have a deep connection and I am able to feel it through the author's words. I would definitely recommend this book over and over.<br><br>There is not much of a cliffy as there was in the first book. We are just left to poner <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Brynne's sudden illness as well as a stranger in the mist <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. <br><br>I love Ethan and Brynne, well maybe just Ethan a little bit more!<br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/image_zpsa6633b48.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br>BR with my lovelies -Barb and Jxxx<br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_450754498" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/450754498" />
    <a title="Anas Attic  Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3178980-anas-attic-book-blog"><img alt="Anas Attic  Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1357693818p2/3178980.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/450754498?book_show_action=true">Nov 07, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anas Attic  Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anas Attic  Book Blog" href="/user/show/3178980-anas-attic-book-blog">Anas Attic  Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3178980-anas-attic-book-blog?shelf=smut-romance">smut-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3178980-anas-attic-book-blog?shelf=auto-buy-author">auto-buy-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3178980-anas-attic-book-blog?shelf=after-fifty-shades">after-fifty-shades</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer450754498" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17327483421791593559">Read more of my reviews and ramblings at <a href='http://www.anas-attic.com/anas_diary' rel='nofollow noopener'>Ana's Attic Book Blog</a><br/><br/>When Raine Miller sent me the ARC of All In (The Blackstone Affair #2), I kind of freaked. I mean this week had some of the best releases ever, but I really wanted to read this and get the review up by release day. Yet I felt like I had to re-read Naked (The Blackstone Affair #1) first. I needed to get back in the zone, you know? In this case, because the first book was fairly short, it was kind of easy to do, except for all the times</span>
  <span id="freeText17327483421791593559" style="display:none">Read more of my reviews and ramblings at <a href="http://www.anas-attic.com/anas_diary" rel="nofollow noopener">Ana's Attic Book Blog</a><br><br>When Raine Miller sent me the ARC of All In (The Blackstone Affair #2), I kind of freaked. I mean this week had some of the best releases ever, but I really wanted to read this and get the review up by release day. Yet I felt like I had to re-read Naked (The Blackstone Affair #1) first. I needed to get back in the zone, you know? In this case, because the first book was fairly short, it was kind of easy to do, except for all the times I had to stop (during both books) for this: <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396862ra/765371.gif" alt="" width="250" height="102" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I’ll tell you this, I loved Naked just as much, if not more, the second time around. All In begins where Naked ends, but this time it is told in Ethan’s voice. It begins a little differently than the preview in Naked, and you will see why. It was an interesting choice on Raine’s part to write the entire novel from the guy's POV. As much as we always love to read that, I must say, I kind of enjoy Brynne’s voice more, because I connect more to her as a female. I mean it was interesting to get inside a man’s head, because we all know what’s in there:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396862ra/765372.gif" alt="" width="108" height="139" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I kept wondering how much research Raine did on how guys think. Did she have help? Is this really how men think? Is that why my husband does that? Sometimes my questions took me out of the story a bit, but maybe because I didn’t feel as ALL IN it as the first book. BUT, that being said, I still loved the crap out of it and can’t wait for the next book. Ideally to me, it will have BOTH points of view, and that would make for a great, unique series.<br><br>When All In begins, Brynne has just left Ethan in his office after finding out they didn’t meet by accident. It is clear Ethan is a mess and totally in love with Brynne. He will do anything to get her back. When they finally talk, Brynne spills the details of what happened to her in the past, which was different than what I expected, and worse in many ways. She thinks Ethan won’t want her anymore if he knows, but this guy is in it for the long haul:<br><br><b>
  <i>“If you come with me, you’re signing on for all of me, Brynne. I don’t know any other way to be with you. It’s All In for me. And I want it to be All In for you too.”</i>
</b><br><br>Ethan is surprised at the depth of his feelings. He is over the top jealous, possessive and controlling, but he reigns it in for her sake. Some of the thoughts through his head were funny though:<br><br><i>
  <b>“I am sure I cut the side of my tongue from gritting my teeth together. The urge to reply back was something I want to do so badly I could taste it next to the tang of blood in my mouth–along the lines of: </b>
</i><b>Sod off, you idiot tosser. She’s taken and her man will cut off your balls if you so much as think about her naked. -Ethan w/the big knife.”</b><br><br>It was clear throughout the story that Ethan needed Brynn’s reassurance that she wouldn’t run away again. She’s done it twice, and he can’t get over the fear that she’ll be gone. Couple that with the fear that someone may be after her, he is swamped with the Olympics, someone may be threatening his cousin, he has a business to run and can’t keep his mind off Brynne, and you have a stressed out guy. But one who is clearly crazy about his girl and will do anything for her.<br><br>And really, would you mind that?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/475866.gif" alt="" width="320" height="240" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Likes:</b><br><br>-The male POV made it a unique and interesting read.<br>-It was longer than the first book.<br>-The sex scenes were still hot as hell.<br>-The Homage to Fifty Shades made me crack up.<br>-Ethan’s dirty talk (and mind).<br><br><b>Dislikes:</b><br><br>-I would have liked to see a little of Brynne’s POV.<br>-Though I liked that it was longer, parts in the middle seemed a bit stretched.<br>-I would like to hear more about Ethan’s past.<br>-This one seemed a little more reminiscent of other popular series out there especially with the mention of Dom/sub.<br>-There was a consistency problem with his smokes, one minute he is smoking more than ever, and one minute he cut back because of Brynne. Since -these ciggies were mentioned a lot, I had to bring this up.<br>-Since Ethan is British, he used words I wasn’t familiar with, and I had to lose my momentum to look them up (plus the word spunk is yuck). But the accent I picture is HOT!<br><br>Rating: 4.5 stars, 5 for Heat<br><br>This is definitely a second book of three. It gets us solid with the characters, gets over the first main conflict, and moves us to the final installment. I like the way Brynne settled into the relationship and doesn’t seem ready to run. She seems ready to forge a healthy relationship. Though it is clear that Ethan is dominant, as soon as he acknowledged that he was a Dom it made the book feel a little too much like all the others. He can be a controlling alpha without the Dom title.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396862ra/765373.gif" alt="" width="250" height="135" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>All in all (see what I did there?) I really enjoyed this book. It was refreshing to read a man’s POV, but I missed Brynne a little. Even though this was still essentially her story through Ethan’s eyes, I missed her. I really loved her character in both books, and I can’t wait for more of this couple!<br><br>Look for the final book in the series Eyes Wide Open, hopefully by the end of the year, and The Rothvale Legacy about Ivan next year.<br><br>*Book was provided by Raine Miller for a fair review<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="17327483421791593559" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_468084272" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/468084272" />
    <a title="Isabella Francesca" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11357561-isabella-francesca"><img alt="Isabella Francesca" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1366728763p2/11357561.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/468084272?book_show_action=true">Dec 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Isabella Francesca" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Isabella Francesca" href="/user/show/11357561-isabella-francesca">Isabella Francesca</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11357561-isabella-francesca?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer468084272" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10044624782435066959"><b>THAT.IS.SO.GOOOOOOOD</b><br/><br/>I don't know about you people, BUT I LOVE IT!!!!! <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399448ra/772976.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><b>“I know you’re scared but I want you to give us a chance anyway. You’re not meant to be alone. You’re meant to be with me.”</b><br/><br/>Sigh. I have no idea where to start...<br/>Since I didn't made any review with the first book <i>(because I was such in a hurry to start the second one)</i>, I'd like to keep this short and simple.<br/><br/>First off: If you are a big fan of Fifty Shades of Grey Series, Crossfire series, On Dublin Street, Insufferable proximity</span>
  <span id="freeText10044624782435066959" style="display:none"><b>THAT.IS.SO.GOOOOOOOD</b><br><br>I don't know about you people, BUT I LOVE IT!!!!! <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399448ra/772976.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>“I know you’re scared but I want you to give us a chance anyway. You’re not meant to be alone. You’re meant to be with me.”</b><br><br>Sigh. I have no idea where to start...<br>Since I didn't made any review with the first book <i>(because I was such in a hurry to start the second one)</i>, I'd like to keep this short and simple.<br><br>First off: If you are a big fan of Fifty Shades of Grey Series, Crossfire series, On Dublin Street, Insufferable proximity (or a book that has a very dominant, possessive, jealous, millionaire hero) then you're good to go with this one.<br><br>IF NOT, then.....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399448ra/772977.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><br>Let me start that Ethan Blackstone is your typical dominant protective alpha-male hero who you are totally going to fall for. She meets little miss damsel in distress, Brynne Bennett and story basically goes from there...<br><br><br>I have to give props for Ms. Raine Miller for doing a good job in writing the story from a man's POV. It's refreshing and different. I personally love it because we get to see what's inside a guy's pea brain for once. Hallelujah!<br><br><br><br>Okay going back, this book for me contains a lot <i>(and really, A LOT)</i> of sex. <br><br><span>[image error]</span> <br><br>I mean, he gets pissed at her then they end up having...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399448ra/772979.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She gets pissed at him again, they end up doing...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399448ra/772980.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He's happy to see her, gets an instant hard on and so they have to....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399448ra/772981.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She wakes up from some weird dream and so she's like....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399448ra/772982.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Damn it, he said "i love you" then she said "i love you" so again <i>(yes you got that right)</i> they did it again!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399448ra/772983.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><br>Yes, it's crazy. Even so, the book still makes sense <i>(unlike the others that's a lot more like porn than a book)</i> and the story just makes you all excited on what's going to happen next <i>(albeit more sex?)</i>. Especially with what really happened to our beloved Mr. Blackstone <i>(but I wanna know more of his past!! Please let there be more explanation on the 3rd one)</i>. But I guess having the book written from his POV gave us a better understanding to his background, how his protective mind works around the woman he loves <i>(which made me fall in love with him even more... le sigh).</i> <br><br>Although the end isn't as shazam as the first book, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[(btw, I really think Brynne is pregnant) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>I am still eager to read it and cannot wait to see how their story ends.<br><br><br><br><i>And that is all. I'm still kind of high with all the Ethan I just read. *swoons*</i><br><br>With that, I leave you with one of my favorite quotes from the book:<br><br><b>
  <i>"They make you believe things that are not true. They tell you so many times, you accept what they are telling you is the truth rather than lies. You suffer for it like it’s the truth. The most effective torture is not physical—it is mental of course. The mind can imagine terrors far more horrific than you could ever physically bear, just like the mind will tune out those physical hurts when the pain surpasses what your body can endure. </i>
</b><br><br><br>X<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="10044624782435066959" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('nfSumbFCKn7Q96nYiXCUBhot/wzK3Veukxxuzl28IFLW4h2NtZyNoacA/ssYKWkR32yT2LvT1wG4l0TJU/YRUQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Vp9t4M89XvhxQ0fe71wg0OghE/df+D4T4dIB2ORmAqAdid70y+P5Jwa0EM1+Bd3HLWB/Iy72vrzKWSvf6iwzow==')})
  }
//]]>

<span id="freeTextContainer5435775009233176882">Raine Miller has been reading romance novels since she picked up that first Barbara Cartland book at the tender age of thirteen. And it's a safe bet she'll never stop, because now she writes them too! Granted Raine's stories are edgy enough to turn Ms. Cartland in her grave, but to her way of thinking, a hot, sexy hero never goes out of fashion. A former teacher, she's now writing sexy romance sto</span>
  <span id="freeText5435775009233176882" style="display:none">Raine Miller has been reading romance novels since she picked up that first Barbara Cartland book at the tender age of thirteen. And it's a safe bet she'll never stop, because now she writes them too! Granted Raine's stories are edgy enough to turn Ms. Cartland in her grave, but to her way of thinking, a hot, sexy hero never goes out of fashion. A former teacher, she's now writing sexy romance stories full time. She has a handsome prince of a husband, two brilliant sons, and two bouncy Italian Greyhounds to pull her back into the real world if the writing takes her too far away. Her sons know she likes to write stories, but gratefully have never asked to read any, thank God! Raine loves to hear from readers and to chat about the characters in her books. You can contact her at raine_miller@ymail.com or visit <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.RaineMiller.com">www.RaineMiller.com</a> to sign up for updates and her newsletter with links to upcoming books. Join us on Facebook at the Raine Miller Romance Readers group here: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/groups/rainemillerreadalong">https://www.facebook.com/groups/raine...</a></span>
